You can easily adjust the preview box just by dragging the split bars.\r\nClean Mode: Double click the picture to start the clean mode, the program will hide menu area and all the functional areas.\r\n\r\nOther functions:\r\nSupports 40 image filters including Blurring, Sharpening, Embossing, Diffusing, Color Balance, and more.
